							<div class="copy"><p>When you find yourself in a new environment and time zone, decisions can sometimes be overwhelming. Add jet-lag, planning where to go and what to do, figuring out what to eat at an over-the-top buffet can trigger your deepest fears of missing out.</p>

			</h3>
							<div class="copy"><p>At the start of your travels, your biggest priorities tend to be packing, not forgetting your ID and actually making your flight. With self-care being hard enough on land, it’s probably a lower priority at 30,000 feet. Staying well when flying in a hermetically sealed air conditioner is probably somewhere lower on your list.</p>

<div class="user-content-block">
<div class="je_rdata_container je_html">
<div class="je_rdata">
<p>Nestled in the heart of modern Amman, Abdali, the past meets the future and the traditions and history of Jordan are instilled with an unmistakably bold design. Enter the hotel through an intriguing canyon walk, a breathtaking recreation inspired by the ancient city of Petra, one of the Seven Wonders of the World.</p>

</div>  <div class="curator-load-more-button-wrapper">
    <button class="curator-load-more-button cta link" type="button" data-load="10" data-max="45">
      Load More    </button>
  </div>

  <script>
    var visiblePosts = parseInt('10');
    var maxPosts = parseInt('45');
    var buttons = document.getElementsByClassName("curator-load-more-button");
    var totalPosts = 10;
    
    for (let index = 0; index < buttons.length; index++) {
      const button = buttons[index];
      button.onclick = function(e) {showNextRow(e)};
    }

    function showNextRow(e) {
      visiblePosts = visiblePosts + parseInt(e.currentTarget.getAttribute('data-load'));
      
      // hide the button if all posts are loaded
      if(visiblePosts >= maxPosts) {
        e.currentTarget.style.display = 'none';
      }

      // collect all the cards
      var cards = Array.from(e.currentTarget.parentElement.previousElementSibling.children);

      // toggle card classes
      updateVisiblePosts(visiblePosts, cards)
      
    }

    function updateVisiblePosts(visiblePosts, cards) {
      cards.forEach(function (card, idx) {
        if(idx < visiblePosts) {
          card.classList.remove('curator-card-hidden')
        }
      });
    }
  </script>
